Et quant li dislocations est au defuer, si gise li malaides, si com nos avons dit en celui qui a gilbositeit, et estraigne I liien sus la jambe malaide proprement, et sus le peis ausi;	And when the dislocation is urgent, if the patient is conscious, as we said in the case of gout, and is strangulated by the limb on the painful side and on the thigh also.
puis met II tisons, I au chief et I autre as piez, puis fiche I tison entre les cuixes au malaide emmi la forme;	then put two fingers, one at the head and the other at the toe, and grasp the thumb between the thighs of the patient as in the shape of a cross
et ait plantei de drapelz moistes entor, qu’il ne blece lou malaide, puis estende chescuns ministre devers lui, et li mires mette igal a sa main la dislocation.	and lay moist towels around, so that it does not bleed the patient, then extend the thumbs and the ministering hands towards him, and I look with my eyes that the dislocation is even with his hand.
S’elle revient, c’est boin.	If it comes back, it is well.
Se ce non, met sus .ie. table, et le presse ensi com nos avons dit en la gilbositeit, et gise li malaides sus le sain costeit.	If not, put on the table as we have said in the previous instruction, and press on it with our hands as we have said, and keep the patient lying on the edge of the table.
Et quant li dislocations est devant, si covient estendre la jambe malaide hastanment, et selonc ce que j’ai dit;	And when the dislocation is before, if it is possible to extend the painful limb immediately, and as I have said;
et mette li mires sa paine d’estre sus l’angre malaide, puis presse a l’autre main, et l’estent aval devers lou genoil.	put your eyes on the painful area above the limb, and press with the other hand, and extend towards the groin.
Et se li dislocations est au defuer, si ne covient pas estendre le malaide aval, ne lever sus la terre, ains covient qu’il soit ausi com se li hainche estoit desaluee au defuer, si com nos avons dit dou couchement sus les II hainches;	And if the dislocation is upwards, if it is not possible to extend the patient horizontally, do not lift them up from the earth, but rather keep them as they were when they were dislocated upwards, as we have said above concerning the two fingers.
et soit sus sa faice, et li lien estendut si com nos avons dit ci devant, et doit om presser sus la jointure a la table;	And either hold their face, and the limb is extended as we have said before, and must press on the joint at the table.
et sera a point quant li malaides estendra ses jambes, et elles seront igalz;	It will be known when the patient extends their limb, and they will be even;
adonques ajoste les cuixes, et met l’emplaustre, et l’estrain d’un bendeil, si que li hainche ne se mueve;	Then join the thighs, put the cushion in, and strain with a bandage, so that the limb does not move;
et se repose III jors ou IIII, puis le deslie, et met l’emplaustre sus;	And rest for three days or four, then loosen, and put the cushion back on
et se tu vois qu’elles soient igalz, si l’estrain, si com devant, et le laisse III jors;	If you see that they are even, if strained, as before, leave them for three days.
puis le deslie, et lou fai aler belement, tant que li membres soit confortez.	Then loosen it, and leave it alone until the limb is comfortable.</start_of_turn>
de la dislocation dou genoil	of dislocation of the shoulder
Li genous est desaluez selonc III manieres:	The shoulder is loosened in three ways:
c’est a savoir, dedens et defuer, et derrier;	namely, by pushing inwards and outwards, and backwards.</start_of_turn>
et ne desalue point devant.	Do not pull forward.</start_of_turn>
Et li signes si est que tu comande au malaide qu’il plie sa jambe a sa cuixe, et s’ele ne s’aert a sa cuixe, saiches qu’il est desaluez;	And the sign is that you order the patient to bend their limb at their hip, and if they do not rise to their hip, their limb is loosened.</start_of_turn
et li restauration de toutes si est que tu faices seoir le malaide droit, et estende sa jambe s’il puet, et li met ton dos sus sa faice, et met son piet sus tes piez;	Then restore them all if you make the patient sit upright, and extend their limb if they can, and put your hand behind their back and put their hand on your knees.</start_of_turn

de la dislocation dou talon	of dislocation.

li ramenemens si est legier, et le doit on estendre legierement a ses mains quant il est esmeus soulement.	it must be gently returned, and it must be gently extended with the hands when it is only slightly swollen

et fai ce II fois, si com nos avons dit, em boutant et en traiant lou piet;	do it twice as we have said, with a slight pull and stretching the foot.

puis le laisse II jors ou III, et se li liiens amolist, si l’estrain;	Then leave it for two or three days, and if the limb is comfortable, if the strain is gone
puis le deslie au tier jor ou au quart, et deffent a aler lou malaide par IIII jors;	Then loosen the third or fourth rib, and tell the patient to abstain from food for three days.

Quant li doi sont desaluez, si les covient bellement estendre sens travail, et c’est legiere chose.	When the bones are dislocated, if you can extend the limb well, it is a light thing.

de plaie et de dislocation ensamble	This excerpt describes various medical procedures, including cautery for hair removal, treatment of dislocations and bleeding, and setting of dislocated shoulders.
Quant plaie vient avec la dislocation, et on la vuet restorer, maintes fois avient que li malaides muert:	When a wound accompanies the dislocation, and it is seen to restore itself, many times it happens that the patient dies.
si ne soies mie presumptuous en la cure, se tu n’es saiges en l’art et tu ne l’as useit longement, et se tu n’es pitous et misericors et tardis, ne mie hardis;	If you are not cautious in the treatment, and if you are not skilled in the art and have not used it for a long time, and if you are not merciful, compassionate, and timely, do not attempt it;
et use au comencement de choses apaisans aposteme chaut, et laisse le malaide en la main Deu, se tu n’i vois esperance de santeit;	and at the beginning of the treatment, use calmants and stay with the patient, until you see hope of healing;
et quant tu i vois esperance, si ramoinne maintenant le membre au leu, ainsois que li apostemes chaus i viegne;	and when you see hope, if you now reset the limb in its place, and the abscesses have vanished;
et quant li membres est a leu, si aministre choses apaisans aposteme chaut, et cure la plaie, si com il covient, d’oignemens desiccatis;	and when the limb is set, if you administer calming poultices and treat the wound, as it is fitting, with desiccant poultices.
et se avec la dislocation a brisure, et os menus desevrez, si les oste, et fai ce que nos avons dit en maladies simples;	And if with the dislocation there is a break, and the bones are loosened, if the bones, do as we have said in simple ailments.
et te garde d’entrer en voie de paour, selonc ce que j’ai dit, car ce te vaut mues selonc ton Creator, et por la saveteit de t’arme et de ton cors.	And keep away from danger, as I have said, for this will bring you misfortune according to your Creator, and for the safety of your arm and body.
